| 1:37:07| I'll take the honor of reading this resolution into the record tonight.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5827)|
| 1:37:14| As someone who has a family member with autism, it's near and dear to my heart,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5834)|
| 1:37:18| and I appreciate the Commission supporting this in full.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5838)|
| 1:37:21| The resolution reads,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5841)|
| 1:37:22| Whereas the first National Autism Awareness Month was launched in April of 1972| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5842)|
| 1:37:28| by the Autism Society due to lack of knowledge of the general public regarding autism,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5848)|
| 1:37:33| and whereas autism is a complex, lifelong developmental disability| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5853)|
| 1:37:38| that typically appears during early childhood and can impact a person's social skills,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5858)|
| 1:37:43| communication, relationships, and self-regulation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5863)|
| 1:37:46| and whereas autism is defined by a certain set of behaviors| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5866)|
| 1:37:50| and is a spectrum condition that affects people differently and to varying degrees,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5870)|
| 1:37:55| and whereas while there is currently no known single cause of autism,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5875)|
| 1:37:59| early diagnosis helps a person receive the support and services that they need,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5879)|
| 1:38:04| which can lead to a quality of life filled with opportunity.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5884)|
| 1:38:07| And whereas more than 3.5 million Americans live with an autism spectrum disorder| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5887)|
| 1:38:13| with approximately 1 in 54 births resulting in an autism spectrum disorder diagnosis,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5893)|
| 1:38:19| and whereas the Knox County Commission wishes to raise public awareness of autism spectrum disorder| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5899)|
| 1:38:25| and express Knox County's commitment to provide support mechanisms for those with this disorder.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5905)|
| 1:38:31| Now, therefore, be it resolved by the Commission of Knox County as follows.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5911)|
| 1:38:35| Knox County Commission hereby recognizes April 2021 as Autism Awareness Month in Knox County| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5915)|
| 1:38:42| and encourages all citizens to help raise awareness and show support for individuals, families, parents,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5922)|
| 1:38:48| teachers, and the many others whose lives are touched by autism.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5928)|
| 1:38:52| Be it further resolved that if any notifications are to be made to effectuate this resolution,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5932)|
| 1:38:57| then the county clerk is hereby requested to forward a copy of this resolution to the proper authority,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5937)|
| 1:39:03| and be it further resolved that this resolution is to take effect from and after its passage| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5943)|
| 1:39:08| as provided by the Charter of Knox County, Tennessee, the public welfare requiring it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5948)|
| 1:39:12| We appreciate all those who are working hard on autism and all the families who are working through it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=5952)|

| 1:44:17| a safe, affordable, stable place to live.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6257)|
| 1:44:20| And as all of you know, these are difficult times in the housing market for all families,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6260)|
| 1:44:25| and so it is just more important than ever that we take steps to recognize Fair Housing Month,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6265)|
| 1:44:30| so I'm glad to read this proclamation on behalf of the mayor.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6270)|
| 1:44:33| A proclamation on behalf of the people of Knox County to publicly recognize Fair Housing Month,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6273)|
| 1:44:38| whereas the Congress of the United States of America passed the Fair Housing Act,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6278)|
| 1:44:43| Title VIII of the Civil Rights Act of 1968,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6283)|
| 1:44:46| which guarantees the rights of individuals to equal housing opportunity,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6286)|
| 1:44:51| and whereas the month of April is recognized by federal, state, and local governments as Fair Housing Month,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6291)|
| 1:44:57| and in recognition, these governments are joined by property owners and managers,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6297)|
| 1:45:02| realtors, financial institutions, landlords, tenants, and all those committed to the equality of our country's citizens| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6302)|
| 1:45:10| and the importance of their fundamental moral and constitutional rights,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6310)|
| 1:45:14| which prohibit, among other things, discrimination in housing on the basis of race or color,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6314)|
| 1:45:20| national origin, religion, sex, familial status, or disability,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6320)|
| 1:45:26| and whereas Knox County supports fairness and equal opportunity in housing| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6326)|
| 1:45:31| to ensure our community's positive and successful social, cultural, and economic growth and development,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6331)|
| 1:45:38| and now, therefore, I, Glenn Jacobs, Knox County Mayor,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6338)|
| 1:45:41| do hereby proclaim April 2021 as Fair Housing Month in Knox County, Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/co-com-r-267-210426?start=6341)|
